So GT = 6.266345790929248·ε·T² - 4288.08·ε·T + 2.353524517872731·ε² + 733908·ε

- Contains ε·T² term (quadratic in T times ε)
- Contains ε·T term (linear in T times ε)
- Contains ε² term
- Contains ε term
- No constant term independent of ε (when ε=0, GT=0)
